- [2026-06-20 +04] fix(rider-app): customer got DUPLICATE "rider picked up" message — regression from the sendCurrentLocation() I added to doPickup. Diagnosis (prod data): unique index ix_outbox_messages_idempotency_key IS enforced; only ONE cust-picked_up-17 row exists (status sent) — so NOT a duplicate enqueue, it's ONE row DELIVERED TWICE. Cause: doPickup fired an explicit first GPS ping that raced with the background GPS task's near-simultaneous ping; both were treated as "first ping" (record_rider_app_location reads last_location_at IS NULL before either commits) → both endpoint calls ran deliver_pending on the same pending row before it was marked sent → sync delivery (_deliver_one) is NOT atomically claimed → WhatsApp send fired twice. FIX (app): removed sendCurrentLocation() from doPickup — the background task's first ping reveals the customer on-the-way+track link exactly once (~5s). Kept sendCurrentLocation() in doDelivered (safe: not a first ping; needed for the live-GPS gate). LATENT/known follow-up (pre-existing, not mine): _deliver_one has no atomic claim, so any two concurrent deliver_pending on the same row could double-send (e.g. two background pings both first). Low likelihood now; harden later via atomic claim if it recurs. tsc clean. Needs APK rebuild. — Removes the double customer pickup message.

- [2026-06-20 +04] fix(rider-app): "delivered stop stays on screen" on device. FIX: import all 13 model modules at the top of apps/workers/celery_app.py (same canonical list as alembic/env.py + tests/conftest.py) so the worker's SQLAlchemy MetaData is complete and the FK resolves. - [2026-06-11 17:30] RENDER DASHBOARD BLANK-PAGE FIX (user: "Dashboard ... its blank page"). ROOT CAUSE: SecurityHeadersMiddleware (src/app/middleware/security.py) sent `Content-Security-Policy: default-src 'none'` on ALL non-/simulator responses. Now that FastAPI serves the built React SPA from the same origin (single-service Render deploy), that CSP made the BROWSER block the page's own /assets/index-*.js and *.css -> #root stayed empty -> blank white page. KEY DIAGNOSTIC TRAP: every prior httpx/curl check returned 200 with correct content-type because non-browser clients DO NOT enforce CSP; only a real browser does. Confirmed via headless Playwright (system Chrome channel) which surfaced: "Loading the script ... violates the following Content Security Policy directive: default-src 'none'". FIX: path-based CSP in the middleware — /simulator keeps its inline-allowing CSP; /api,/webhooks,/health,/metrics,/openapi,/docs,/redoc stay strict default-src 'none'; everything else (the SPA: /, /login, /assets, ...) gets a functional CSP: default-src 'self'; script-src 'self'; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' https://fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' data: https://fonts.gstatic.com; img-src 'self' data: blob: https:; connect-src 'self'; frame-ancestors 'none'; base-uri 'self'. The fonts.googleapis/gstatic + img https: allowances are REQUIRED because frontend/src/styles/fonts.css @imports Google Fonts and OrderDetailDrawer.tsx loads OpenStreetMap tiles. TDD: tests/obs/test_security_headers.py +2 tests (SPA path allows self scripts + fonts + tiles & is NOT default-src 'none'; API paths stay strict); full security-headers file 6 passed, ruff clean. Needs commit+push -> Render auto-deploy to take effect live.

Both steps best-effort (try/except + rollback) so a dispatch/delivery error never breaks the kitchen action. Runs in the web request that marks ready — no celery beat needed. ## 2026-07-20 22:30 — Fix: staff PIN login bounced back to /login (401 → global logout)
  - Root cause: staff-audience JWT (aud=staff) 401'd on GET /api/v1/me, and TopBar (in AppShell) calls /me on EVERY guarded screen; apiClient interceptor treats any 401 as session-expired → clears token + window.location.assign('/login'). POS reads (/menus/active, /orders) were also owner-only → same bounce for cashier/waiter on /new-order.
  - Fix (backend): added current_restaurant_any dep in src/app/staff/deps.py — accepts owner (aud=manager) OR any staff PIN token (aud=staff, resolves tenant via staff.restaurant_id). Read-only shell/POS context.
  - Wired current_restaurant_any onto: GET /api/v1/me (identity/router.py), GET /api/v1/menus/active (menu/router.py), GET /api/v1/orders list (ordering/router.py)
  - Order-taking endpoints now require_role("manager","cashier","waiter") instead of owner-only current_restaurant: /manual/customer-lookup, POST /manual, POST /pos
  - Verified live: staff id1/pin1234 (role=manager) → /me 200, /orders 200 (were 401). /menus/active 404 only because local DB has no active menu (data, not auth) — POS shows "No active menu" banner, no bounce.
  - Import-checked (no circular import: identity/menu/ordering routers import staff.deps; staff.deps imports only identity.auth/models + staff.models).
  - Local run note: .env APP_DATABASE_URL points to a remote Render DB (dpg-... host, unresolvable locally + malformed double scheme). Run backend with APP_DATABASE_URL=postgresql+asyncpg://app:app@localhost:5433/restaurant against docker postgres. Uvicorn --reload can leave an inherited-socket zombie holding :8000 on Windows; started without --reload.

## 2026-07-20 23:10 — Fix: clicking any sidebar item logged cashier out (whole class of 401→logout)
  - Root cause: many tenant-scoped endpoints still guard with owner-only current_restaurant, which raised 401 "invalid token" for a VALID staff PIN token. apiClient interceptor treats any 401 as session-expiry → clears token + redirects /login. So every cashier-allowed screen (Customers, Floor, Payments...) bounced.
  - PRIMARY fix (src/app/identity/deps.py): current_restaurant now returns 403 (not 401) when the bearer is a VALID staff token lacking manager access; only a genuinely invalid/expired token yields 401. 403 is not in the frontend interceptor → no logout. Universal safety net for the whole class.
  - Opened high-value cashier reads to any authenticated actor (current_restaurant_any): GET /api/v1/ordering/customers (list + /{id} detail), GET /api/v1/tables. Writes/loyalty/mutations stay owner-only.
  - Verified live cashier (id2/pin1234): /me 200, /orders 200, /ordering/customers 200, /tables 200, /menus/active 404 (no menu seeded), /tickets 403, /payments/credentials 403 — NO 401 anywhere → no bounce.
  - Security note: current_restaurant still authorizes (staff without manager access → 403). Endpoints on bare current_restaurant remain manager-only; per-role opening done deliberately per endpoint. Consider auditing remaining current_restaurant endpoints vs ROUTE_ROLE_MAP for staff-allowed screens (payments drawer for cashier still 403 on credentials/billing — those are manager config, acceptable).
